

.. Transportation:

Transportation
====================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================

How do people move from place to place?

.. contents::
   :local:
   :depth: 10





.. _au.data.B46_Tot_P:

Total (Persons)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------





Method of Travel to Work





Measure "Total (Persons)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B46_Tot_P'
      );





Measure "Total (Persons)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
          'au.data.B46_Tot_P'
        );






Measure "Total (Persons)" percent of "Total (Persons)" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B46_Tot_P',
        'denominator'
      );


Measure "Total (Persons)" percent of "Total (Persons)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
        'au.data.B46_Tot_P',
        'denominator'
      );

One method Bicycle (Persons)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^





Method of Travel to Work





Measure "One method Bicycle (Persons)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B46_One_method_Bicycle_P'
      );





Measure "One method Bicycle (Persons)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
          'au.data.B46_One_method_Bicycle_P'
        );






Measure "One method Bicycle (Persons)" percent of "Total (Persons)" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B46_One_method_Bicycle_P',
        'denominator'
      );


Measure "One method Bicycle (Persons)" percent of "Total (Persons)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
        'au.data.B46_One_method_Bicycle_P',
        'denominator'

""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""





Method of Travel to Work





Measure "One method Car as driver (Females)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131),
        'au.data.B46_One_method_Car_as_driver_F'
      );

.. code-block:: postgresql

        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(-33.8806, 151.2131), 0.01),
          'au.data.B46_One_method_Car_as_driver_F'
        );

.. code-block:: postgresql
